***sprookje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sprookje.html>sprookje</a> (6839)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">sproke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">obsolete variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spreuk.html>spreuk</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-je</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Note that the word only occurs in this diminutive form; the word "sprook" does not exist (except as a <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> back-formation for comedic effect).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>fairy tale
<ol><li>a usually old, allegorical short story</li>
<li>story presented as true that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not believable</li></ol></li>
<li>dream come true <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">very desirable life</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***spruit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spruit.html>spruit</a> (38895)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sprute</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spruut</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spruyte</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sprite</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sprout</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spruit.html>spruit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spruiten.html>spruiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spruitje.html>spruitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sprout, shoot, a branch-like part of a plant which grows from the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a></li>
<li>A child, seen as a parent's offspring, usually <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of a minor</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">construction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A style or beam which rests on another</li>
<li>A branch of a plumbing pipe, rope etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small river, river branch, especially used in South African toponyms</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spoyte</i>, probably related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spuien.html>spuien</a></i>.

***spuitgast.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spuitgast.html>spuitgast</a> (112765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spuit.html>spuit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spout, hose, nozzle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gast.html>gast</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guest, guy, dude</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spuitgast.html>spuitgast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spuitgasten.html>spuitgasten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spuitgastje.html>spuitgastje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">firefighter</span>, especially a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, who operates a <span class="Latn" lang="en">firehose</span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Rarely this job title may be interpreted gender-neutrally and be used to refer to a female firefighter. However, due to the association of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gast.html>gast</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with males, typically <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">brandweervrouw</i> will be used in such <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Brandweermens</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a fully gender-neutral alternative.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">brandspuitgast</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerman.html>brandweerman</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">brandweervrouw</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">brandweermens</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">spuitmeester</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:spuitgast.html>spuitgast</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speciaal.html>speciaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgeleid.html>opgeleid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brandweer.html>brandweer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestrijden.html>bestrijden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></li></ol>

***sputnik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> sputnik (19577)</h1><br></body> 
***sputter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sputter.html>sputter</a> (72752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably representing <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*sputren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*sputrien</i>, a frequentative form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sputen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spout, vomit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spout</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">spüttern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to inject, spray, splash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">sputterje</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sputter.html>sputter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">sputteren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sputter.html>sputter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">sputtern</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">spruttern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sprinkle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">sprudeln</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spout, squirt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="Latn" lang="en">splutter</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sputter.html>sputter</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sputters</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Moist matter thrown out in small detached particles.</li>
<li>Confused and hasty speech.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sputter.html>sputter</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">sputters</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sputtering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sputtered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To emit saliva or spit from the mouth in small, scattered portions, as in rapid speaking.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1869</b> May,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Trollope" class="extiw" title="w:Anthony Trollope">Anthony Trollope</a>,  “Lady Milborough as Ambassador”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/He_Knew_He_Was_Right" class="extiw" title="w:He Knew He Was Right">He <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>Knew</a> He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> Right</a></cite>, volume I, London |  Strahan and Company, publishers,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="56, Ludgate Hill, London">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/1118026626">1118026626</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=Sb4BAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA87">page 87</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The child [...] kicked, and crowed, and <b>sputtered</b>, when his mother <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> him, and put up his little <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> to clutch her hair, and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> to her as a young <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a> upon the earth. Nothing in the world <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> ever <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> created so beautiful, so joyous, so satisfactory, so divine!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive, intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To speak so rapidly as to emit saliva; to utter <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> hastily and indistinctly, with a spluttering sound, as in rage.
<ul><li><b>1700</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Congreve" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Congreve">William Congreve</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Way_of_the_World" class="extiw" title="s:The Way of the World">s:The Way of the World</a></i>
<dl><dd>They could neither of them speak their rage, and so fell a <b>sputtering</b> at one another, like two roasting apples.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1730</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Swift" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jonathan Swift"><a href = vnd.unilang:jonathan.html>Jonathan</a> Swift</a>, <i>A Vindication of Lord Carteret</i>
<dl><dd>In the midst of caresses, and without the least pretended incitement, to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sputter.html>sputter</a></b> out the basest and falsest accusations.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive, intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To throw out anything, as little <a href = vnd.unilang:jets.html>jets</a> of steam, with a noise like that made by one sputtering.
<ul><li><b>1692</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, <i>Cleomenes, the Spartan Hero, a Tragedy</i>
<dl><dd>Like the green wood [...] <b>sputtering</b> in the flame.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cause surface atoms or electrons of a solid to be ejected by bombarding it with heavy atoms or ions.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To coat the surface of an object by sputtering.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spuugt.html>spuugt</a> (14194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spuugt.html>spuugt</a></strong>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:squared.html>squared</a> (87906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:squared.html>squared</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">simple past tense and past participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">square</i></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:squared.html>squared</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Covered with a grid  of <a href = vnd.unilang:squares.html>squares</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Raised to the second power.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>When used attributively in the mathematical sense and applied to a phrase representing a mathematical or physical quantity, the adjective <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually postpositive, as in “3 <a href = vnd.unilang:squared.html>squared</a> plus 4 <a href = vnd.unilang:squared.html>squared</a> equals 5 squared”.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="None" lang="mul">²</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">square</span></li></ul>
</body>

***squawk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:squawk.html>squawk</a> (67356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown <span class="defdate">[from 1821]</span>, but probably of imitative origin (compare dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">squacco</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small-crested heron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:squawk.html>squawk</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">squawks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A shrill noise, especially made by a voice or bird; a yell, scream, or call.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A four-digit <a href = vnd.unilang:transponder.html>transponder</a> code used by aircraft for identification or transmission of emergency signals.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An issue or complaint related to aircraft maintenance.
<ul><li><b>1969</b>, <i>American Aviation</i> (volume 32)
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> think instructors should stress the importance of writeups on all maintenance <b>squawks</b> after the completion of each flight. More important, something should be done by the aircraft operator to correct such <b>squawks</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The American night heron.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">programming<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A warning message indicating a possible error.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  Scott Meyers,  <cite>Effective C++ Digital Collection: 140 Ways to Improve Your Programming</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The function-hiding code above, for instance, goes through a different (but widely used) compiler with nary a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:squawk.html>squawk</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:squawk.html>squawk</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">squawks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">squawking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">squawked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make a squawking noise; to yell, scream, or call out shrilly.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1945</b> August 17,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Orwell" class="extiw" title="w:George Orwell">George Orwell</a> [pseudonym; <a href = vnd.unilang:eric.html>Eric</a> Arthur Blair],  chapter 6, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Animal_Farm" class="extiw" title="w:Animal Farm">Animal Farm: A Fairy Story</a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harvill_Secker" class="extiw" title="w:Harvill Secker">Secker amp; Warburg</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3655473">3655473</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:hens.html>hens</a> woke up <b>squawking</b> with terror because they <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> all dreamed simultaneously of hearing a gun go off in the distance.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To speak out; to protest.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To report an infraction; to <a href = vnd.unilang:rat.html>rat</a> on or tattle; to disclose a secret.
<ul><li><b>1948</b>, Andrew <a href = vnd.unilang:geren.html>Geer</a>, <i>The Sea Chase</i> (page 68)
<dl><dd>"I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> slit your throat if you <b><a href = vnd.unilang:squawk.html>squawk</a></b> on us," <a href = vnd.unilang:krantz.html>Krantz</a> threatened.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">programming<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To produce a warning message, indicating a possible error.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1993</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:steve.html>Steve</a> Maguire,  <cite>Writing Solid Code</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">That way, if you type = instead of ==, the compiler will <b><a href = vnd.unilang:squawk.html>squawk</a></b> because you can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> assign something to a constant.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2013</b>, Bill Sempf, ‎Chuck Sphar, ‎Stephen <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Davis, <i>C 5.0 All-in-One For <a href = vnd.unilang:dummies.html>Dummies</a></i>
<dl><dd>You want the compiler to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:squawk.html>squawk</a></b> if you try to instantiate for a type that doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> implement IPrioritizable.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To set or transmit a four-digit <a href = vnd.unilang:transponder.html>transponder</a> code. <span class="use-with-mention">(Normally followed by the specific code in question.)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To back out in a mean way.</li></ol>

***staal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:staal.html>staal</a> (4671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stael</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stāl</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stahal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stahlą</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:stahl.html>Stahl</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">stål</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">stál</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">steel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiel.html>stiel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staal.html>staal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">steel</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stalen.html>stalen</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">made of steel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stael</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*stalo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stalô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">staff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">steel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staal.html>staal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stalen.html>stalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staaltje.html>staaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sample
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:staal.html>staal</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarde.html>waarde</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">worthless <b>sample</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***staan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a> (273)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stâen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stān</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stāną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stand, to be upright
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>Dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stond.html>stond</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gisteren.html>gisteren</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:supermarkt.html>supermarkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a>...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">So I <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> standing</b> in supermarket yesterday and then...</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be, to be placed or located
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In Holland <b><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">In Holland there <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> a house.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms a continuous aspect. Although it <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> an implication of standing, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> vague and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not strictly required or emphasized.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sta.html>sta</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koken.html>koken</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What <b>are</b> you cooking there?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say, to be written, to be <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to be indicated in written form</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grondwet.html>grondwet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kabinet.html>kabinet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verantwoordelijk.html>verantwoordelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beleid.html>beleid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>koning</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onschendbaar.html>onschendbaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the constitution <b>it says</b> that the cabinet <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> responsible for governance and that the king <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inviolable.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suit, fit, befit (of clothing)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <b>suits</b> you!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> (375)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stat</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stedi</i> (whence <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>stede</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stee</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stadiz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stéh₂tis</i>.
</p><p>The plural <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> preserved the old Germanic <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> in a morphological function, a rarity in Dutch. Several derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> have <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> as well.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>steden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stadje.html>stadje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>city, town</li>
<li>the town/city centre
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am now in <b>town</b>. I am now in the centre (of town).</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></b> in.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am going into <b>town</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stadia.html>stadia</a> (35603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:staking.html>staking</a> (10708)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staken.html>staken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>. First attested in the sixteenth century.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staking.html>staking</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stakingen.html>stakingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staking.html>stakinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>strike <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">work stoppage</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li>cessation, delay, the act of ending or delaying something</li>

***stal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stal.html>stal</a> (2597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stal.html>stal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:stal.html>stal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stallaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stal.html>stal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stallen.html>stallen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stalletje.html>stalletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stable, a place to keep hoofed animals</li>
<li>stall, notably as a vending place on a market</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marked period of time</li>
